    "/api/gateway/Orders/{orderNumber}/lines/{lineNo}/discount": {
      "put": {
        "tags": [
          "Orders"
        ],
        "summary": "Applies or replace a discount to an order line in an existing order and  returns this order",
        "parameters": [
          {
            "name": "orderNumber",
